ARIE vol.055, 1932-1933


A. List of copper-plates examined during the year 1932-33.
1
Placement
The Collector of Tanjore
Year
Vijayana-gara.
King
Śrīraṅgadēva-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1574 (expir-ed), Nandana,Tai 21, Monday,Uttiraṭṭādi, śu.pañchamī.
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks
The plate belongs to the Trusteeof the Kailāsanātha temple atMolaiyūr, Kumbakonam taluk.The characters are too modernfor the date cited. Names ofcertain Vijayanagara kings aregiven without any order.Purports to register an agree-ment made among the resident-merchants of several villages ofthe Pandanallūr-śīrmai to payimposts at certain rates perhead-load on grains and otherarticles of merchandise, forproviding for the daily offeringsand worship in the templeof Kailāsanāthasvāmi andSaundariyammaṉ at Muḻaiyūr.
2
Placement
The Zamindar of Punganur,through the Collector ofChittoor.
Year
Suguṭūru
King
Immaḍi Chikkarāya Tam-maya-Gaunayya.
Date
Śaka 1648, Plava,Vaiśākha, śu. 5.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
Records the agreement given tothe chief by the Reḍḍis,Karṇams, Śeṭṭis and the 18phaṇas of the several villages(in his estate), settling in cashthe amount of annual rent tobe paid by each village on itstobacco crops.
3
Placement
Do.
Year
Do.
King
Mummaḍi Chikkarāya
Date
Śaka 1725, Rudhi-rōdgāri, Śrāvaṇa,ba. 30, Wednes-day, solar eclipse.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
Refers to the chief as the son ofImmaḍi Chikkarāya and Dēvī-rammaṇṇi (the daughter ofVūlapāṭi Raṅgēgaunivāru) andthe grandson of MummaḍiChikkarāya of the Sadāśiva-gōtra. Registers an endow-ment of lands made by thechief for the daily and specialworships, offerings and lampsin the temple of Śiva built byhim near Bhīmapuram attachedto the Mōdugulapalle-sthala,and also the construction of atank by him in the same place.Registers also the chief'srenovation of the village-tankto the south of the temple, andhis foundation of a garden nearits bund. Records a supple-mentary gift of land made bythe chief in Dhātu, on Āśvija,śu. 10, to the same temple.
4
Placement
The Zamindar of Punganur,through the Collector ofChittoor.
Year
Suguṭūru
King
Chikkarāya Tammaya-Gaunivāru.
Date
Śaka 1598, Naḷa,Śrāvaṇa, śu. 12.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
The letters are too modern for thedate given in the record andare also indifferently engraved.Purports to register a cowlgiven by the chief to fourpersons granting as dasavandamhalf of the produce on the landsirrigated by a tank dug bythem at Sōmulavirigi-pēṇṭa-sthala in Āvulapalle-sīma. Theinscription bears at the end thesignature ‘Chikarāyalu’.
5
Placement
Do.
Year
Do.
King
Immaḍi Chikkarāya
Date
Śaka 1675, Śrī-mukha, Māgha,śu, 10.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
Refers to the chief as the grand-son of Suguṭūru ImmaḍiChikkarāya of the Sadāśiva-gōtra and the son of MummaḍiChikkarāya and his wifeMañjammaṇṇi, the daughter ofLiṅgana-Gaunivāru of Baira-kūru. Registers the gift oflands made by the chief for theseveral services and festivals inthe temple of Śiva (Mṛityuñ-jayēśvara) built by him atChauḍēpalle.
6
Placement
Do.
Year
Do.
King
Mummaḍi Chikkarāya
Date
Śaka 1722, Raudri,Māgha, śu. 15,Thursday.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
Refers to the chief as the grand-son of Suguṭūru MummaḍiChikkarāya of the Sadāśiva-gōtra and the son of ImmaḍiChikkarāya and his wifeDēvīrammaṇṇi who was thedaughter of Vūlapāṭi Raṅgē-Gaunivāru. Registers the con-struction of a Śiva (Chandra-śēkharasvāmin) temple anda tank near Rāmasamudramby the chief and the endow-ment of lands made by him tothe same temple.
7
Placement
Mr. S.T.Srinivasagopala-chari, B.A., M.L., Advocate,Madras.
Year
EasternChāḷukya.
King
Vishṇuvardhana-Mahārāja
Date
...... Uttarā-yaṇa.
Language and Script
Sanskrit (in Chāḷukyan characters)
Remarks
This is an odd plate of a set theremaining plates of which aremissing. Refers to the king'sfather Maṅgi-Yuvarāja by thetitle Abhilashitakārya-Vijaya-siddhi. Registers the tax-freegrant of a land sowable with 12khaṇḍikas of kōdrava seedmade by the king to the scholarVṛiddha-śarman well-versed inthe three Vēdas, who was theson of Rēva-śarman and grand-son of Śaṅkara-śarman of theHārīti-gōtra and Āpastamba-sūtra and was a resident ofVaṅgipaṟu.
8
Placement
Do.
Year
Vijaya-nagara.
King
Achyutadēva-Mahārāya
Date
Śaka 1459, Hēma-lamba, Kārttika,śu. Utthāna-dvādaśī.
Language and Script
Sanskrit (in Nāgarī)
Remarks
Registers the sarvamānya grantof the village Śeruvañjūrurenamed Achyutēndramahā-rāyapuram situated in Nandi-vala-sīma in Kōnādi-nāḍu, asubdivision of Reṇḍāyiravēlip-paṟṟu in Śeṅgāṭṭu-kōṭṭam, adistrict in the Chandragiri-rājyaof Jayaṅkoṇḍachōḷa-maṇḍalam,divided into shares amongseveral learned Brāhmaṇas ofvarious gōtras and sūtras. Thegrant is said to have beenmade by the king in thepresence of God Viṭṭhalēśvaraon the bank of the Tuṅga-bhadrā, at the request ofTimmappa-Nāyaka.
9
Placement
Mr. T. Krishna Aiyangar,Village Munsiff, Kollan-kondan, Srivillipputturtaluk, Ramnad district.
Year
LaterPāṇḍya.
King
Jaṭilavarman alias Tribhu-vanachakravartin Kōnē-[ri]ṉmaikoṇḍāṉ AbhirāmaAtivīrarāma Śrīvallabha.
Date
19th year, Śaka1503, Vṛisha,Uttarāyaṇa, Grī-shma-ṛitu,Mithuna 24, ba.5, Wednesday,Śatabhishaj,Saubhāgya-yōga,Taitila-karaṇa.
Language and Script
Sanskrit in Grantha
Remarks
Registers the grant made byAbhirāma-Sundarēśa Vara-tuṅgarāma, who was the son ofKulaśēkharadēva Parākrama-Pāṇḍyadēva of the Ātrēya-gōtra and was born in thePushya-nakshatra, of thevillage Śōlaiśēri alias Nayinā-ragaram in Āṇmaṟai-nāḍu, asan agrahāra to Brāhmaṇas ofvarious gōtras and sūtras, underthe new name Śivakāma-sundari-chaturvēdimaṅgalamgiven to it in honour of hisqueen. Refers to the donor'selder brother Guṇarāma.

Remarks

Year
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1073, Uttarā-yaṇa-saṅkrānti.
Language and Script
Sanskrit & Telugu
Remarks
Refers to Origāṇḍi Rēmana of the Śrīvatsa-gōtra whowas the minister of king Rājēndra-Chōḍa and wasappointed by him the governor of Kamma-dēśa. Hisson was Drōṇa, whose son by his wife Prōlāmbikā wasKumāra (called also Komma) who was the minister ofGoṅka, the son of Chōḍa (i.e. Rājēndra-Chōḍa).Komma is stated to have built the temple ofKumārēśvara and constructed the tank calledDrōṇasamudra at Nārāyaṇapāḍu. Registers the grantof lands made for the offerings of the god and toBrahmans, and the gift of 55 sheep for a perpetuallamp to the god Sōmēśvaradēva of the village, by thesame minister who is called also Mandadi Kommanā-mātya who is styled the ‘lord of the town ofOrigāṇḍi.’

On another slab built into thewall of the same temple.

Qutb-Shāhi

Śaka 1514 [Na]nda-na, Vaiśākha, śu.3, Thursday.
Language and Script
Telugu (prose & verse)
Remarks

Soon afterthe march of the officer from Gōlakoṇḍa, the rebelsdispersed and the chief, crossing the river Kṛishṇā,entered the sīma and reduced them to subjection.

Stone standing in SurveyNo. 276.
Year
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1726, Raktāk-shi, Adhika-Chait-ra, śu. 15.
Language and Script
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records a gift of land made by Dēsāyi Bahadar Liṅ-gappa-Gauḍa, son of Bahadar Hanumanta-Gauḍa andgrandson of Bahadar Liṅgappa-Gauḍa of Guttaḷal, toŚivarāya-Jōyisa, son of Jayarāma-Śāstri and grandsonof Śivarāya-Jōyisa, the court astronomer (Sadara-Jōyisa) of Hāvanūr, who belonged to the Kāśyapa-gōtra and studied the Āśvalāyana-sūtra of the Ṛik-śākhā. The donor is stated to be born of the Mauna-Bhārgava-gōtra and belonged to the Kaṇva-śākhā ofthe Āpastamba-sūtra of the Śukla-Yajurvēda.
3
Placement
Stone lying in Survey No. 272
Year
WesternChāḷukya.
King
Jagadēkamalladēva (II)
Date
…
Language and Script
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records the erection of a Śivālaya by the wife of Amita-ṛishi of Kōḍiyabīḍu and registers a gift of land madeby Māreya-Nāyaka, ‘son’ (putra) of Amitarāśi-Jīya,to the temple of Bāchēśvaradēva, during the regimeof Mahāprabhu Bācha-Gāvuṇḍa of the Ka[daṁba]-kula, when Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Tailapadēva wasgoverning Banavāsi Twelve Thousand and administer-ing the ubhaya-sāmya. Also registers a gift of landmade to the mason Dēvaja who constructed thesukanāsi of the temple with bricks and rendered minorservice in the temple of Bāchēśvara, while Jakki-Śeṭṭi,son of Chīli-Śeṭṭi was enjoying the Śeṭṭitana ofKōḍiyabīḍu.

5
Placement
Stone standing near the temple ofBasavaṇṇa in Survey No. 240.
Year
WesternChāḷukya.
King
Tribhuvanamalladēva
Date
Chāḷukya-Vikramayear 40, Manma-tha, Paushya,amāvāsya, MondayUttarāyaṇa-saṅk-rānti, solar eclipse,Vyatīpāta.
Language and Script
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Badly damaged. Registers a gift of land, by purchase,made by Birudaradēva, a subordinate of Baṅ[ki]-yarasa, who was administering Beḷgahe Seventy,[Palasige]......Iṭṭage Thirty ...... groups of villagesin Banavāse Twelve Thousand ...... and the agrahāravillages Savaṇūru, Savasi, Kundugōḷa, etc., from hiscapital at Agaṇḍeya-bīḍu (modern Agaḍi), to thetemple of Birudēśvaradēva built by him at Agaṇḍe.The gift was entrusted to the care of Varēśvara-Paṇḍita disciple of Vādidēva-Munipa. Also recordsminor gifts made to the same temple by the NagaraFive Hundred and the Telliga Fifty (communities).

10
Placement
Dēvagēri.--Broken slab built intothe tīrthakuṇḍa in the templeof Yellamma.
Year
Kaḷachurya.
King
Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Tribhu-vanaikavīra Bijjaṇadēva.
Date
Śaka 1082, Vikrama,Chaitra, śu. 1,Monday, Uttarā-yaṇa-saṅkrānti,Vyatīpāta.
Language and Script
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Damaged. Registers a gift of land made by HeggaḍeBammarasa for the merit of his sister Lachchaladēvīto Rāmasiṅgi-Paṇḍita, for offerings etc., in the templeof Grāmēśvaradēva (?) at Tammuge, when Māchidēva-rasa of the Khēchara-vaṁśa and the Jīmūtavāhan-ānvaya was administering Bāsavura One Hundred andForty, and Sēnādhipati Kariya-Kēsimayya was govern-ing Banavāsi Twelve Thousand. Also records othergifts made to the same temple by Suṅkādhikāri Māyi-dēvarasa, the Sixty families of Tammuge, the UguraThree hundred and other communities.

32
Placement
Stone-pillars of a makara-tōraṇain the same temple.
Year
WesternChāḷukya.
King
Traiḷōkyamalladēva
Date
Śaka 984, Śubhakṛit,Phālguṇa, śu. 13,Thursday.
Language and Script
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Records the construction of a makara-tōraṇa to thegoddess Māḻajadēvī at Deyvada Posavūru (i.e. Dēviho-sūr), by Aṅgharakka Indapayya-Nāyaka, whenMahāmaṇḍalēśvara Chāvuṇḍarāyarasa was governingBanavāsi Twelve Thousand, and his son MahāsāmantaJōmadēvarasa was administering Bāsavūru One Hund-red and Forty, Beḷmahe Seventy and Sattaḷige Seventy,and the latter's subordinate Lōkanāthayya was thePerggaḍe of the Three Hundred and Seventy (divisions)and Rājādityarasa of the Jimūtavāhana lineage washolding the office of nāḻgāmuṇḍa of Bāsavura OneHundred and Forty, and the One Thousand (Mahā-janas) of the agrahāra village Deyvada-Posavūru wereprotecting the village.

Placement
Broken slab standing in the sametemple.

King
Siṅgaṇadēva
Date

34
Placement
Another slab in the same temple
Year
WesternChāḷukya.
King
Pratāpachakravartin Jagadēka-malladēva (II) ‘ruling fromthe nelevīḍu at Kalyāṇa-pura’.
Date
10th year, Vibhava,Pushya, ba. amā-vāsye, Sunday, Ut-tarāyaṇa-saṅkrānti,Vyatīpāta, solareclipse.
Language and Script
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Damaged at the end. Registers a gift of taxes made bythe Suṅkādhikāri Dēvadhara-Daṇḍanāyaka for thebenefit of the temple of the goddess Māḷachidēvi atHosavūr in Bāsavūr One Hundred and Forty, a divi-sion of Banavāsi Twelve Thousand province, whenDaṇḍanāyaka Rēcharasa who was governing the latterfrom Baḷḷigrāme, had gone there to fulfil the vow(harake) to the deity. Mentions Kaliyammarasa of theKhachara lineage. Also records gifts of land madefor the same goddess to Mādhavadēva and for thetanks Hiriyakeṟe and Gejjegeṟe by the Mahānāḍuand the village assemblies.

Damaged. In characters of the 12th centuryA.D. Gives a verse in praise of Chandrabhūshaṇa-[vratin].
192
Placement
Kōṭavumachgi.--Broken stonelying in the temple of Sōmēś-vara.
Year
WesternChāḷukya.
King
Bhūlōkamalladēva
Date
…
Language and Script
Kannaḍa
Remarks
Fragment. Mentions Ummachige as an agrahara inNareyaṅgal [Twelve] included in Beḷvala, and refersto the Brahman Māhaṇāryya, the brother of Padmaṇaand son of Jēmaṇa born in the Chānura-vaṁśa.
NAVALGUND TALUK
